</p>

***inshallah.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:inshallah.html>inshallah</a> (57143)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">Ø¥ÙÙÙ Ø´ÙØ§Ø¡Ù Ù±ÙÙÙÙ°Ù</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Ê¾in Å¡ÄÊ¾a llÄh</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:inshallah.html>inshallah</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> willing; <a href = vnd.unilang:deo.html>Deo</a> volente; expressing the speakerâs wish for a given future event to occur, especially in a Muslim country or Islamic context.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> will sign the contract tomorrow, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:inshallah.html>inshallah</a></b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In many contexts, including military <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a>, the expression <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sarcastic, suggesting that the speaker <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> no interest in making the future event occur (thus, it will only occur if <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:steps.html>steps</a> in and wills it).</li>
<li>In Arab countries <a href = vnd.unilang:inshallah.html>inshallah</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often added to any sentence in the future tense. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> to show that the future event <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not assured and if <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>'s will <a href = vnd.unilang:steps.html>steps</a> in, it will not happen. I wish the event <a href = vnd.unilang:happens.html>happens</a>, but I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> have it all in my hands and unpredictable can happen. I wish it <a href = vnd.unilang:happens.html>happens</a>, but if it's not <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>'s will, it will not happen.</li></ul>
</body>

***inslaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:inslaan.html>inslaan</a> (9212)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaan.html>slaan</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:inslaan.html>inslaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to shatter, to break with force</li>
<li>to turn into, to follow (e.g. a different path or a corner)</li>
<li>to make provision for (e.g. a feast)</li>
<li>to strike with force (e.g. lightning)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">inslÃ¢pen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">inslÄpan</i>; equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slapen.html>slapen</a></i>. ***inspelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:inspelen.html>inspelen</a> (35054)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spelen.html>spelen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:inspelen.html>inspelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to react [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(to)</span></span>], to capitalise [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(on)</span></span>] <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to respond to certain circumstances with action or behaviour</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
